# Commuting squares of homotopies

<pre class="Agda"><a id="44" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="51" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html" class="Module">foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies</a> <a id="99" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Idea

A square of [homotopies](foundation-core.homotopies.md)

```text
          top
      f ------> g
      |         |
 left |         | right
      ∨         ∨
      h ------> i
        bottom
```

is said to be a {{#concept "commuting square" Disambiguation="homotopies"}} of
homotopies if there is a homotopy `left ∙h bottom ~ top ∙h right `. Such a
homotopy is called a
{{#concept "coherence" Disambiguation="commuting square of homotopies" Agda=coherence-square-homotopies}}
of the square.

## Definitions

### Commuting squares of homotopies

### Horizontally constant squares

{{#concept "Horizontally constant squares" Disambiguation="homotopies" Agda=horizontal-refl-coherence-square-homotopies}}
are commuting squares of homotopies of the form

```text
       refl-htpy
    f ----------> f
    |             |
  H |             | H
    ∨             ∨
    g ----------> g.
       refl-htpy
```

### Vertically constant squares

{{#concept "Vertically constant squares" Disambiguation="homotopies" Agda=vertical-refl-coherence-square-homotopies}}
are commuting squares of homotopies of the form

```text
                H
            f -----> g
            |        |
  refl-htpy |        | refl-htpy
            ∨        ∨
            f -----> g.
                H
```

### Squares with refl on the top and bottom

Given a homotopy `H ~ H'`, we can obtain a coherence square with `refl-htpy` on
the top and bottom.

```text
       refl-htpy
    f ----------> f
    |             |
  H |             | H'
    ∨             ∨
    g ----------> g
       refl-htpy
```

href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3116" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="3118" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3118" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="3120" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3088" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3128" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3130" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3132" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3100" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="3134" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3123" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3135" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="3139" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3140" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3140" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="3142" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3142" class="Bound">H&#39;</a> <a id="3145" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3147" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3116" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="3149" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="3151" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3118" class="Bound">g</a><a id="3152" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="3156" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="3165" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3165" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies-horizontal-refl</a> <a id="3209" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="3215" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3140" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="3217" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="3219" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3142" class="Bound">H&#39;</a> <a id="3222" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="3228" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a>
      <a id="3262" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3264" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2724" class="Function">refl-htpy</a><a id="3273" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="3281" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3283" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3140" class="Bound">H</a><a id="3284" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="3292" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3294" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3142" class="Bound">H&#39;</a><a id="3296" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="3304" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3306" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2724" class="Function">refl-htpy</a><a id="3315" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="3319" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3165" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies-horizontal-refl</a> <a id="3363" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3363" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="3365" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="3371" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#5171" class="Function">right-unit-htpy</a> <a id="3387" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#3099" class="Function Operator">∙h</a> <a id="3390" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3363" class="Bound">K</a>
</pre>
Conversely, given a coherence square as above, we can obtain a homotopy
`H ~ H'`.

<pre class="Agda">  <a id="3490" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3490" class="Function">inv-coherence-square-homotopies-horizontal-refl</a> <a id="3538" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="3544" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a>
      <a id="3578" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3580" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2724" class="Function">refl-htpy</a><a id="3589" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="3597" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3599" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3140" class="Bound">H</a><a id="3600" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="3608" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3610" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3142" class="Bound">H&#39;</a><a id="3612" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="3620" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3622" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2724" class="Function">refl-htpy</a><a id="3631" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3633" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="3639" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3140" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="3641" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="3643" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3142" class="Bound">H&#39;</a>
  <a id="3648" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3490" class="Function">inv-coherence-square-homotopies-horizontal-refl</a> <a id="3696" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3696" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="3698" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="3704" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#5244" class="Function">inv-htpy-right-unit-htpy</a> <a id="3729" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#3099" class="Function Operator">∙h</a> <a id="3732" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#3696" class="Bound">K</a>
</pre>
### Squares with `refl-htpy` on the left and right

Given a homotopy `H ~ H'`, we can obtain a coherence square with `refl-htpy` on
the left and right.

```text
                 H'
            f ------> g
            |         |
  refl-htpy |         | refl-htpy
            ∨         ∨
            f ------> g
                 H
```

## Operations

### Inverting squares of homotopies horizontally

Given a commuting square of homotopies

```text
           top
       f -------> g
       |          |
  left |          | right
       ∨          ∨
       h -------> i,
          bottom
```

the square of homotopies

```text
              top⁻¹
        g ------------> f
        |               |
  right |               | left
        ∨               ∨
        i ------------> h
             bottom⁻¹
```

commutes.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="5245" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="5252" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5252" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="5256" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5257" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5257" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="5260" id="5277" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="5280" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5257" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="5282" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5284" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5285" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5285" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="5287" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5289" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5260" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="5298" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5300" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5301" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5301" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="5303" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5303" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="5305" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="5328" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="5337" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5337" class="Function">horizontal-inv-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="5380" class="Symbol">:</a>

    <a id="5510" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="5538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5539" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2897" class="Function">inv-htpy</a> <a id="5548" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5387" class="Bound">top</a><a id="5551" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5553" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5416" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="5559" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5401" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="5564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5565" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2897" class="Function">inv-htpy</a> <a id="5574" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5432" class="Bound">bottom</a><a id="5580" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="5584" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5337" class="Function">horizontal-inv-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="5627" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5627" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="5631" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5631" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="5636" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5636" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="5642" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5642" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="5649" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5649" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="5651" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5651" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5653" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="5659" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-identifications.html#4938" class="Function">horizontal-inv-coherence-square-identifications</a>
      <a id="5713" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5715" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5627" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="5719" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5651" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5720" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="5728" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5730" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5631" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="5735" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5651" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5736" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="5744" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5746" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5636" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="5752" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5651" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5753" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="5761" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5763" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5642" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="5770" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5651" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5771" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="5779" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5781" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5649" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="5783" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#5651" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5784" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Inverting squares of homotopies vertically

Given a commuting square of homotopies

```text
           top
       f -------> g
       |          |
  left |          | right
       ∨          ∨
       h -------> i,
          bottom
```

the square of homotopies

```text
            bottom
         h -------> i
         |          |
  left⁻¹ |          | right⁻¹
         ∨          ∨
         f -------> g
             top
```

commutes.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="6243" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6250" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#6250" class="Module">_</a>

      <a id="6771" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6773" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#6643" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="6775" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#6645" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6776" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Functions acting on squares of homotopies

Given a commuting square of homotopies

```text
           top
       f -------> g
       |          |
  left |          | right
       ∨          ∨
       h -------> i
          bottom
```

in `(x : A) → B x`, and given a dependent map `F : {x : A} → B x → C x`, the
square of homotopies

```text
                 F ·l top
           f f -----------> f g
            |                |
  F ·l left |                | F ·l right
            ∨                ∨
            h -------------> i
               F ·l bottom
```

commutes.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="7372" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="7379" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7379" class="Module">_</a>

    <a id="7847" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-identifications.html#6923" class="Function">map-coherence-square-identifications</a>
      <a id="7890" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7892" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7477" class="Bound">F</a><a id="7893" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="7901" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7903" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7815" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="7907" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7839" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7908" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="7916" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7918" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7819" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="7923" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7839" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7924" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="7932" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7934" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7824" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="7940" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7839" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7941" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="7949" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7951" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7830" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="7958" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7839" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7959" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="7967" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7969" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7837" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="7971" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#7839" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7972" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Similarly we may whisker it on the right.

  <a id="8130" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="8521" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#8513" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="8523" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2725" class="Function Operator">·r</a> <a id="8526" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#8511" class="Bound">F</a>

### Concatenating homotopies of edges and coherences of commuting squares of homotopies

Consider a commuting square of homotopies and a homotopy of one of the four
sides with another homotopy, as for example in the diagram below:

```text
             top
       a ---------> b
       |           | |
  left |     right |~| right'
       ∨           ∨ ∨
       c ---------> d.
           bottom
```

Then any homotopy witnessing that the square commutes can be concatenated with
the homotopy on the side, to obtain a new commuting square of homotopies.

**Note.** To avoid cyclic module dependencies we will give direct proofs that
concatenating homotopies of edges of a square with the coherence of its
commutativity is an equivalence.

#### Concatenating homotopies of the top edge with a coherence of a commuting square of homotopies

Consider a commuting diagram of homotopies

```text
           top'
         ------->
       f -------> g
       |   top    |
  left |          | right
       ∨          ∨
       h -------> i.
          bottom
```

with a homotopy `top ~ top'`. Then we get maps back and forth

```text
           top                             top'
       f -------> g                    f -------> g
       |          |                    |          |
  left |          | right    ↔    left |          | right
       ∨          ∨                    ∨          ∨
       h -------> i                    h -------> i.
          bottom                          bottom
```

We record that this construction is an equivalence in
[`foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies`](foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.md).

      <a id="10692" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="10694" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10298" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="10700" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10588" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10701" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="10727" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="10729" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10348" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="10731" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10588" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10732" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="10740" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="10742" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10586" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="10744" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10588" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10745" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="10750" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10750" class="Function">inv-concat-top-homotopy-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="10802" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="10808" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="10836" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10333" class="Bound">top&#39;</a> <a id="10841" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10283" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="10846" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10298" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="10852" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10314" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="10859" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="10865" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="10893" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10269" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="10897" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10283" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="10902" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10298" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="10908" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10314" class="Bound">bottom</a>
  <a id="10917" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10750" class="Function">inv-concat-top-homotopy-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="10969" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10969" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="10971" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10971" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10973" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="10979" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-identifications.html#9291" class="Function">inv-concat-top-identification-coherence-square-identifications</a>
      <a id="11048" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11050" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10269" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="11054" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10971" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11055" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="11063" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11065" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10283" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="11070" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10971" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11071" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="11079" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11081" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10298" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="11087" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10971" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11088" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="11096" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11098" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10314" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="11105" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10971" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11106" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="11114" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11116" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10348" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="11118" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10971" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11119" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="11127" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11129" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10969" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="11131" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#10971" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11132" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
#### Concatenating homotopies of the left edge with a coherence of a commuting square of homotopies

Consider a commuting diagram of homotopies

```text
              top
         f -------> g
        | |         |
  left' | | left    | right
        ∨ ∨         ∨
         h -------> i.
            bottom
```

with a homotopy `left ~ left'`. Then we get maps back and forth

```text
           top                              top
       f -------> g                     f -------> g
       |          |                     |          |
  left |          | right    ↔    left' |          | right
       ∨          ∨                     ∨          ∨
       h -------> i                     h -------> i.
          bottom                           bottom
```

We record that this construction is an equivalence in
[`foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies`](foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.md).

      <a id="13008" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13010" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#12849" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="13012" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#12851" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13013" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
#### Concatenating homotopies of the right edge with a coherence of a commuting square of homotopies

Consider a commuting diagram of homotopies

```text
            top
       f -------> g
       |         | |
  left |   right | | right'
       ∨         ∨ ∨
       h -------> i.
          bottom
```

with a homotopy `right ~ right'`. Then we get maps back and forth

```text
           top                             top
       f -------> g                    f -------> g
       |          |                    |          |
  left |          | right    ↔    left |          | right'
       ∨          ∨                    ∨          ∨
       h -------> i                    h -------> i.
          bottom                          bottom
```

      <a id="14735" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14737" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#14575" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="14739" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#14577" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14740" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
We record that this construction is an equivalence in
[`foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies`](foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.md).

#### Concatenating homotopies of the bottom edge with a coherence of a commuting square of homotopies

Consider a commuting diagram of homotopies

```text
            top
       f -------> g
       |          |
  left |          | right
       ∨  bottom  ∨
       h -------> i.
         ------->
          bottom'
```

with a homotopy `bottom ~ bottom'`. Then we get maps back and forth

```text
           top                             top
       f -------> g                    f -------> g
       |          |                    |          |
  left |          | right    ↔    left |          | right
       ∨          ∨                    ∨          ∨
       h -------> i                    h -------> i.
          bottom                          bottom'
```

      <a id="16230" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16232" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15836" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="16234" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16088" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16235" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="16253" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16253" class="Function">inv-concat-bottom-homotopy-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="16308" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="16314" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="16342" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15754" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="16346" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15768" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="16351" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15783" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="16357" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15818" class="Bound">bottom&#39;</a> <a id="16365" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="16371" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="16399" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15754" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="16403" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15768" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="16408" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15783" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="16414" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15799" class="Bound">bottom</a>
  <a id="16423" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16253" class="Function">inv-concat-bottom-homotopy-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="16478" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16478" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="16480" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16480" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16482" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="16488" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-identifications.html#16561" class="Function">inv-concat-bottom-identification-coherence-square-identifications</a>
      <a id="16560" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16562" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15754" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="16566" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16480" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16567" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="16575" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16577" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15768" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="16582" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16480" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16583" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="16591" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16593" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15783" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="16599" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16480" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16600" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="16608" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16610" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15799" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="16617" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16480" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16618" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="16626" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16628" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#15836" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="16630" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16480" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16631" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="16639" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16641" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16478" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="16643" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#16480" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16644" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
We record that this construction is an equivalence in
[`foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies`](foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.md).

### Whiskering and splicing coherences of commuting squares of homotopies with respect to concatenation of homotopies

Given a commuting square of homotopies

```text
           top
       f -------> g
       |          |
  left |          | right
       ∨          ∨
       h -------> i,
          bottom
```

we may consider four ways of attaching new homotopies to it:

1. Prepending `H : u ~ f` to the left gives us a commuting square

   ```text
                H ∙h top
              u -------> g
              |          |
    H ∙h left |          | right
              ∨          ∨
              h -------> i.
                 bottom
   ```

   More precisely, we have an equivalence

   ```text
     (left ∙h bottom ~ top ∙h right) ≃ ((H ∙h left) ∙h bottom ~ (H ∙h top) ∙h right).
   ```

2. Appending a homotopy `H : i ~ u` to the right gives a commuting square of
   homotopies

   ```text
                   top
           f ------------> g
           |               |
      left |               | right ∙h H
           ∨               ∨
           h ------------> u.
              bottom ∙h H
   ```

   More precisely, we have an equivalence

   ```text
     (left ∙h bottom ~ top ∙h right) ≃ (left ∙h (bottom ∙h H) ~ top ∙h (right ∙h H)).
   ```

3. Splicing a homotopy `H : h ~ u` and its inverse into the middle gives a
   commuting square of homotopies

   ```text
                      top
              f --------------> g
              |                 |
    left ∙h H |                 | right
              ∨                 ∨
              u --------------> i.
                 H⁻¹ ∙h bottom
   ```

   More precisely, we have an equivalence

   ```text
     (left ∙h bottom ~ top ∙h right) ≃ ((left ∙h H) ∙h (H⁻¹ ∙h bottom) ~ top ∙h right).
   ```

   Similarly, we have an equivalence

   ```text
     (left ∙h bottom ~ top ∙h right) ≃ ((left ∙h H⁻¹) ∙h (H ∙h bottom) ~ top ∙h right).
   ```

4. Splicing a homotopy `H : g ~ u` and its inverse into the middle gives a
   commuting square of homotopies

   ```text
            top ∙h H
          f --------> u
          |           |
     left |           | H⁻¹ ∙h right
          ∨           ∨
          h --------> i.
             bottom
   ```

   More precisely, we have an equivalence

   ```text
     (left ∙h bottom ~ top ∙h right) ≃ (left ∙h bottom ~ (top ∙h H) ∙h (H⁻¹ ∙h right)).
   ```

   Similarly, we have an equivalence

   ```text
     (left ∙h bottom ~ top ∙h right) ≃ (left ∙h bottom ~ (top ∙h H⁻¹) ∙h (H ∙h right)).
   ```

These operations are useful in proofs involving homotopy algebra, because taking
`equiv-right-whisker-concat-coherence-square-homotopies` as an example, it
provides us with two maps: the forward direction states
`(H ∙h r ~ K ∙h s) → (H ∙h (r ∙h t)) ~ K ∙h (s ∙h t))`, which allows one to
append a homotopy without needing to reassociate on the right, and the backwards
direction conversely allows one to cancel out a homotopy in parentheses.

#### Left whiskering coherences of commuting squares of homotopies

For any homotopy `H : u ~ f` we obtain maps back and forth

```text
           top                                H ∙h top
       f -------> g                         u -------> g
       |          |                         |          |
  left |          | right    ↔    H ∙h left |          | right
       ∨          ∨                         ∨          ∨
       h -------> i                         h -------> i
          bottom                               bottom
```

of coherences of commuting squares of homotopies. We show in
[`foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies`](foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.md)
that these maps are equivalences.

href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#20561" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="21245" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="21247" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#20565" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21248" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21250" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21251" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21251" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="21258" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21260" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#20563" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="21262" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="21264" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#20565" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21265" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21267" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="21273" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="21301" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21302" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21190" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="21304" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#3099" class="Function Operator">∙h</a> <a id="21307" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21206" class="Bound">top</a><a id="21310" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21312" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21313" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21190" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="21315" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#3099" class="Function Operator">∙h</a> <a id="21318" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21220" class="Bound">left</a><a id="21322" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21324" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21235" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="21330" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21251" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="21337" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="21343" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="21371" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21206" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="21375" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21220" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="21380" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21235" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="21386" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21251" class="Bound">bottom</a>
  <a id="21395" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21113" class="Function">left-unwhisker-concat-coherence-square-homotopies</a>
    <a id="21449" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21449" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="21451" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21451" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="21455" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21455" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="21460" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21460" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="21466" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21466" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="21473" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21473" class="Bound">coh</a> <a id="21477" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21477" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21479" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="21485" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-identifications.html#21740" class="Function">left-unwhisker-concat-coherence-square-identifications</a>
      <a id="21546" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21548" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21449" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="21550" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21477" class="Bound">x</a><a id="21551" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="21559" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21561" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21451" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="21565" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21477" class="Bound">x</a><a id="21566" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="21574" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21576" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21455" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="21581" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21477" class="Bound">x</a><a id="21582" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="21590" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21592" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21460" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="21598" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21477" class="Bound">x</a><a id="21599" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="21607" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21609" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21466" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="21616" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21477" class="Bound">x</a><a id="21617" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="21625" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21627" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21473" class="Bound">coh</a> <a id="21631" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#21477" class="Bound">x</a><a id="21632" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
#### Right whiskering coherences of commuting squares of homotopies

For any homotopy `H : i ~ u` we obtain maps back and forth

```text
           top                                 top
       f -------> g                     f ------------> g
       |          |                     |               |
  left |          | right    ↔     left |               | right ∙h H
       ∨          ∨                     ∨               ∨
       h -------> i                     h ------------> i
          bottom                           bottom ∙h H
```

of coherences of commuting squares of homotopies. We show in
[`foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies`](foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.md)
that these maps are equivalences.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="22386" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="22393" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#22393" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="22397" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22398" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#22398" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="22401"       <a id="23325" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23327" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#22499" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="23333" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#23231" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23334" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="23342" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23344" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#22515" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="23351" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#23231" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23352" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="23360" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23362" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#23225" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="23364" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#23231" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23365" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="23373" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23375" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#23227" class="Bound">coh</a> <a id="23379" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#23231" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23380" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>

      <a id="24142" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24144" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#23922" class="Bound">bottom</a><a id="24150" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="24158" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24160" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#23931" class="Bound">H</a><a id="24161" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="24169" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24171" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#23929" class="Bound">q</a><a id="24172" class="Symbol">))</a>

#### Left splicing coherences of commuting squares of homotopies

For any inverse pair of homotopies `H : g ~ u` and `K : u ~ g` equipped with
`α : inv-htpy H ~ K` we obtain maps back and forth

```text
           top                                    top
       f -------> g                         f -----------> g
       |          |                         |              |
  left |          | right    ↔    left ∙h H |              | right
       ∨          ∨                         ∨              ∨
       h -------> i                         u -----------> i
          bottom                               K ∙h bottom
```

of coherences of commuting squares of homotopies. We show in
[`foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies`](foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.md)
that these maps are equivalences.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="25010" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="25017" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#25017" class="Module">_</a>

    <a id="25212" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25213" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#25213" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="25215" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25217"       <a id="26051" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26053" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#25914" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="26055" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#25924" class="Bound">x</a><a id="26056" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="26064" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26066" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#25916" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="26068" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#25924" class="Bound">x</a><a id="26069" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="26077" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26079" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#25918" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="26081" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#25924" class="Bound">x</a><a id="26082" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="26090" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26092" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#25920" class="Bound">coh</a> <a id="26096" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#25924" class="Bound">x</a><a id="26097" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
#### Right splicing coherences of commuting squares of homotopies

For any inverse pair of homotopies `H : g ~ u` and `K : u ~ g` equipped with
`α : inv-htpy H ~ K` we obtain maps back and forth

```text
           top                             top ∙h H
       f -------> g                     f --------> u
       |          |                     |           |
  left |          | right    ↔     left |           | K ∙h right
       ∨          ∨                     ∨           ∨
       h -------> i                     h --------> i
          bottom                           bottom
```

of coherences of commuting squares of homotopies. We show in
[`foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies`](foundation.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.md)
that these maps are equivalences.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="26894" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="26901" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#26901" class="Module">_</a>

    <a id="27097" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27098" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#27098" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="27100" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27102"     <a id="27168" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="27196" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#26978" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="27200" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#26992" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="27205" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#27007" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="27211" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#27023" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="27218" class="Symbol">→</a>

      <a id="27972" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27974" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#27823" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="27976" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#27831" class="Bound">x</a><a id="27977" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="27985" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27987" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#27825" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="27989" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#27831" class="Bound">x</a><a id="27990" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="27998" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28000" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#27827" class="Bound">coh</a> <a id="28004" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#27831" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28005" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Horizontally pasting squares of homotopies

Consider two squares of homotopies as in the diagram

```text
            top-left         top-right
       a -------------> b -------------> c
       |                |                |
  left |                | middle         | right
       ∨                ∨                ∨
       d -------------> e -------------> f
          bottom-left      bottom-right
```

with `H : left ∙h bottom-left ~ top-left ∙h middle` and
`K : middle ∙h bottom-right ~ top-right ∙h right`. Then the outer square
commutes.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="28575" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="28582" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28582" class="Module">_</a>

    <a id="28929" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="28957" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28682" class="Bound">top-right</a> <a id="28967" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28719" class="Bound">middle</a> <a id="28974" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28736" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="28980" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28776" class="Bound">bottom-right</a> <a id="28993" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="28999" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1155" class="Function">coherence-square-homotopies</a>
      <a id="29033" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29034" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28663" class="Bound">top-left</a> <a id="29043" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#3099" class="Function Operator">∙h</a> <a id="29046" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28682" class="Bound">top-right</a><a id="29055" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29057" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28704" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="29062" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28736" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="29068" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29069" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28754" class="Bound">bottom-left</a> <a id="29081" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#3099" class="Function Operator">∙h</a> <a id="29084" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28776" class="Bound">bottom-right</a><a id="29096" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="29100" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28809" class="Function">horizontal-pasting-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="29147" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29147" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="29149" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29149" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="29151" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29151" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="29153" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="29159" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-identifications.html#29033" class="Function">horizontal-pasting-coherence-square-identifications</a>

      <a id="29237" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29239" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28682" class="Bound">top-right</a> <a id="29249" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29151" class="Bound">x</a><a id="29250" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29258" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29260" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28704" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="29265" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29151" class="Bound">x</a><a id="29266" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29274" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29276" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28719" class="Bound">middle</a> <a id="29283" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29151" class="Bound">x</a><a id="29284" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29292" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29294" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28736" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="29300" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29151" class="Bound">x</a><a id="29301" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29309" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29311" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28754" class="Bound">bottom-left</a> <a id="29323" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29151" class="Bound">x</a><a id="29324" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29332" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29334" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#28776" class="Bound">bottom-right</a> <a id="29347" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29151" class="Bound">x</a><a id="29348" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29356" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29358" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29147" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="29360" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29151" class="Bound">x</a><a id="29361" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29369" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29371" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29149" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="29373" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29151" class="Bound">x</a><a id="29374" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Vertically pasting squares of homotopies

Consider two squares of homotopies as in the diagram

```text
                  top
              a --------> b
              |           |
     top-left |           | top-right
              ∨  middle   ∨
              c --------> d
              |           |
  bottom-left |           | bottom-right
              ∨           ∨
              e --------> f
                 bottom
```

with `H : top-left ∙h middle ~ top ∙h top-right` and
`K : bottom-left ∙h bottom ~ middle ∙h bottom-right`. Then the outer square
commutes.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="29963" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="29970" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#29970" class="Module">_</a>

## Properties

### Left unit law for horizontal pasting of commuting squares of homotopies

<pre class="Agda"><a id="30863" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="30870" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#30870" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="30874" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="30875" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#30875" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="30878" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="30946" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="30955" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#30955" class="Function">left-unit-law-horizontal-pasting-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="31016" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="31022" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31023" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#31023" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="31027" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31029" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#30919" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="31031" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="31033"       <a id="34390" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="34392" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#34243" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="34394" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#34245" class="Bound">x</a><a id="34395" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Computing the right whiskering of a vertically constant square with a homotopy

Consider the vertically constant square of homotopies

```text
           H
       f -----> g
       |        |
  refl |        | refl
       ∨        ∨
       f -----> g
           H
```

at a homotopy `H : f ~ g`, and consider a homotopy `K : g ~ h`. Then the right
whiskering of the above square with `K` is the commuting square of homotopies

```text
            H
       f -------> g
       |          |
  refl |   refl   | K
       ∨          ∨
       f -------> h
          H ∙h K
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="34987" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="34994" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#34994" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="34998" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="34999" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#34999" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="35002" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35002" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="35005" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35007" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="35012" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35014" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35015" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35015" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35017" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35019" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="35022" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#34999" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="35024" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35026" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35027" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35027" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="35029" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35031" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35015" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35033" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35035" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="35038" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35002" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="35040" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35042" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35043" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35043" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="35045" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35045" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="35047" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35047" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="35049" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35051" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35052" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35052" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="35054" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35056" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35015" class="Bound">A</a><a id="35057" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35059" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35061" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35027" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="35063" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35052" class="Bound">x</a><a id="35064" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="35068" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="35077" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35077" class="Function">right-whisker-concat-vertical-refl-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="35140" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="35146" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35147" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35147" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="35149" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35151" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35043" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="35153" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="35155" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35045" class="Bound">g</a><a id="35156" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35158" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35159" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35159" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="35161" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35163" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35045" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="35165" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="35167" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35047" class="Bound">h</a><a id="35168" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35170" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="35176" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#22542" class="Function">right-whisker-concat-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="35225" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35147" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="35227" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2724" class="Function">refl-htpy</a> <a id="35237" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2724" class="Function">refl-htpy</a> <a id="35247" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35147" class="Bound">H</a>
      <a id="35255" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="35257" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#2546" class="Function">vertical-refl-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="35299" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35147" class="Bound">H</a><a id="35300" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="35308" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="35310" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35159" class="Bound">K</a><a id="35311" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35313" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a>
    <a id="35319" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2724" class="Function">refl-htpy</a>
  <a id="35331" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35077" class="Function">right-whisker-concat-vertical-refl-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="35394" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35394" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="35396" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35396" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="35398" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35398" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="35400" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="35406" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-identifications.html#34979" class="Function">right-whisker-concat-vertical-refl-coherence-square-identifications</a>
      <a id="35480" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="35482" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35394" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="35484" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35398" class="Bound">x</a><a id="35485" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="35493" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="35495" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35396" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="35497" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#35398" class="Bound">x</a><a id="35498" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Computing the right whiskering of a horizontally constant square with a homotopy

Consider a horizontally constant commuting square of homotopies

```text
       refl-htpy
    f ----------> f
    |             |
  H |             | H
    ∨             ∨
    g ----------> g
       refl-htpy
```

at a homotopy `H` and consider a homotopy `K : g ~ h`. Then the right whiskering
of the above square with `K` is the square

```text
       refl-htpy
    f ----------> f
    |             |
  H |  refl-htpy  | H ∙h K
    ∨             ∨
    g ----------> h.
           K
```

      <a id="36603" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="36605" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#36504" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="36607" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#36506" class="Bound">x</a><a id="36608" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Computing the left whiskering of a horizontally constant square with a homotopy

Consider a homotopy `H : f ~ g` and a horizontally constant commuting square of
homotopies

```text
       refl-htpy
    g ----------> g
    |             |
  K |             | K
    ∨             ∨
    h ----------> h
       refl-htpy
```

at a homotopy `K : g ~ h`. The the left whiskering of the above square with `H`
is the commuting square

```text
                                    K ∙h refl-htpy
         f -----------------------------------------------------------------> g
         |                                                                    |
  K ∙h H | right-unit-htpy ∙h (right-whisker-concat-htpy right-unit-htpy H)⁻¹ | H
         ∨                                                                    ∨
         h -----------------------------------------------------------------> h.
                                      refl-htpy
```

    <a id="38208" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38209" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38209" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="38211" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38213" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#37625" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="38215" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="38217" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#37627" class="Bound">g</a><a id="38218" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38220" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38221" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38221" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="38223" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38225" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#37627" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="38227" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="38229" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#37629" class="Bound">h</a><a id="38230" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38232" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="38238" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#20595" class="Function">left-whisker-concat-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="38286" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38209" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="38288" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2724" class="Function">refl-htpy</a> <a id="38298" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38221" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="38300" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38221" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="38302" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2724" class="Function">refl-htpy</a>
      <a id="38318" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="38320" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#1847" class="Function">horizontal-refl-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="38364" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38221" class="Bound">K</a><a id="38365" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38367" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a>
    <a id="38373" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#5171" class="Function">right-unit-htpy</a> <a id="38389" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#3099" class="Function Operator">∙h</a> <a id="38392" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2897" class="Function">inv-htpy</a> <a id="38401" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38402" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies-concatenation.html#2334" class="Function">right-whisker-concat-htpy</a> <a id="38428" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#5171" class="Function">right-unit-htpy</a> <a id="38444" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38221" class="Bound">K</a><a id="38445" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="38449" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38137" class="Function">left-whisker-concat-horizontal-refl-coherence-square-homotopies&#39;</a> <a id="38514" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38514" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="38516" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38516" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="38518" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38518" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="38520" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="38526" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-identifications.html#37619" class="Function">left-whisker-concat-horizontal-refl-coherence-square-identifications&#39;</a>
      <a id="38602" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="38604" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38514" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="38606" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38518" class="Bound">x</a><a id="38607" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="38615" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="38617" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38516" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="38619" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#38518" class="Bound">x</a><a id="38620" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Computing the left whiskering of a vertically constant square with a homotopy

Consider the vertically constant square of homotopies

```text
                K
            g -----> h
            |        |
  refl-htpy |        | refl-htpy
            ∨        ∨
            g -----> h
                K
```

at a homotopy `K : g ~ h` and consider a homotopy `H : f ~ g`. Then the left
whiskering of the above square with `H` is the square

```text
                                            H ∙h K
                 f ----------------------------------------------------------> h
                 |                                                             |
  H ∙h refl-htpy | right-whisker-concat-htpy right-unit-htpy K ∙h right-unit⁻¹ | refl-htpy
                 ∨                                                             ∨
                 g ----------------------------------------------------------> h.
                                              K
```

      <a id="40635" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="40637" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#40538" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="40639" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#40540" class="Bound">x</a><a id="40640" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Left whiskering horizontal concatenations of squares with homotopies

Consider a commuting diagram of homotopies of the form

```text
            top-left        top-right
       a -------------> c -------------> e
       |                |                |
  left |                | middle         | right
       ∨                ∨                ∨
       b -------------> d -------------> f
          bottom-left      bottom-right
```

and consider a homotopy `H : f ~ a`. Then the left whiskering of `H` and the
horizontal concatenation of coherences of commuting squares is up to
associativity the horizontal concatenation of the squares

```text
               H ∙h top-left      top-right
            u -------------> c -------------> e
            |                |                |
  H ∙h left |                | middle         | right
            ∨                ∨                ∨
            b -------------> d -------------> f
               bottom-left      bottom-right
```

where the left square is the left whiskering of `H` and the original left
square.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="41733" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="41740" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41740" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="41744" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41745" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41745" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="41748" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41748" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="41751" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41753" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="41758" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41760" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41761" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41761" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="41763" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41765" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="41768" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41745" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="41770" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41772" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41773" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41773" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="41775" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41777" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41761" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="41779" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41781" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="41784" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41748" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="41786" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="41799" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41799" class="Function">left-whisker-concat-horizontal-pasting-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="41866" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="41872" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41873" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41873" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="41875" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41875" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="41877" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41877" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="41879" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41879" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="41881" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41881" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="41883" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41883" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="41885" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41885" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="41887" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41889" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41890" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41890" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="41892" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41894" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41761" class="Bound">A</a><a id="41895" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41897" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41899" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41773" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="41901" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41890" class="Bound">x</a><a id="41902" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41904" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41905" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41905" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="41907" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41909" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41873" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="41911" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="41913" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41875" class="Bound">a</a><a id="41914" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="41920" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41921" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41921" class="Bound">top-left</a> <a id="41930" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41932" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41875" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="41934" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="41936" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41879" class="Bound">c</a><a id="41937" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41939" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41940" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41940" class="Bound">top-right</a> <a id="41950" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41952" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41879" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="41954" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="41956" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#41883" class="Bound">e</a><a id="41957" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="43276" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="43278" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43100" class="Bound">top-right</a> <a id="43288" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43157" class="Bound">x</a><a id="43289" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="43331" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="43333" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43122" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="43339" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43157" class="Bound">x</a><a id="43340" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="43348" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="43350" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43128" class="Bound">bottom-left</a> <a id="43362" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43157" class="Bound">x</a><a id="43363" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="43371" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="43373" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43140" class="Bound">bottom-right</a> <a id="43386" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43157" class="Bound">x</a><a id="43387" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="43395" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="43397" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43153" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="43399" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43157" class="Bound">x</a><a id="43400" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="43408" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="43410" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43155" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="43412" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#43157" class="Bound">x</a><a id="43413" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Left whiskering vertical concatenations of squares with homotopies

Consider two squares of homotopies as in the diagram

```text
                  top
              a --------> b
              |           |
     top-left |           | top-right
              ∨  middle   ∨
              c --------> d
              |           |
  bottom-left |           | bottom-right
              ∨           ∨
              e --------> f
                 bottom
```

and consider a homotopy `H : f ~ a`. Then the left whiskering of `H` with the
vertical pasting of the two squares above is up to associativity the vertical
pasting of the squares

```text
                  H ∙h top
                u --------> b
                |           |
  H ∙h top-left |           | top-right
                ∨  middle   ∨
                c --------> d
                |           |
    bottom-left |           | bottom-right
                ∨           ∨
                e --------> f.
                   bottom
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="44428" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="44435" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#44435" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="44439" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44440" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#44440" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="44443" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#44443" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="44446" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44448" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="44453" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="44455" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44456" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#44456" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="44458" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44460" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="44463" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#44440" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="44465" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="44467" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44468" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#44468" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="44470" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44472" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#44456" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="44474" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="44476" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="44479" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#44443" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="44481" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="44485" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="44494" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#44494" class="Function">left-whisker-concat-vertical-concat-coherence-square-homotopies</a> <a id="44558" class="Symbol">:</a>

      <a id="46025" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="46027" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#45808" class="Bound">bottom-right</a> <a id="46040" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#45832" class="Bound">x</a><a id="46041" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="46049" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="46051" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#45821" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="46058" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#45832" class="Bound">x</a><a id="46059" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="46067" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="46069" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#45828" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="46071" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#45832" class="Bound">x</a><a id="46072" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="46080" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="46082" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#45830" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="46084" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#45832" class="Bound">x</a><a id="46085" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Right whiskering horizontal pastings of commuting squares of homotopies

Consider a commuting diagram of homotopies of the form

```text
            top-left        top-right
       a -------------> c -------------> e
       |                |                |
  left |                | middle         | right
       ∨                ∨                ∨
       b -------------> d -------------> f
          bottom-left      bottom-right
```

and consider a homotopy `K : f ~ g`. Then the right whiskering of the horizontal
pasting of the squares above is up to associativity the horizontal pasting of
the squares

```text
            top-left           top-right
       a -------------> c ------------------> e
       |                |                     |
  left |                | middle              | right ∙h K
       ∨                ∨                     ∨
       b -------------> d ------------------> g
          bottom-left      bottom-right ∙h K
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="47067" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="47074" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#47074" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="47078" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="47079" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#47079" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="47082" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#47082" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="47085" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="47087" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="47092" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="47094" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="47095" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#47095" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="47097" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="47099" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="47102" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#47079" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="47104" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="47106" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="47107" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#47107" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="47109" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="47111" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#47095" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="47113" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="47115" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="47118" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#47082" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="47120" class="Symbol">}</a>
