      <a id="48740" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="48742" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#48508" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="48744" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#48514" class="Bound">x</a><a id="48745" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="48753" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="48755" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#48510" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="48757" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#48514" class="Bound">x</a><a id="48758" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="48766" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="48768" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#48512" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="48770" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#48514" class="Bound">x</a><a id="48771" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Right whiskering vertical concatenations of squares with homotopies

Consider two squares of homotopies as in the diagram

```text
                  top
              a --------> b
              |           |
     top-left |           | top-right
              ∨  middle   ∨
              c --------> d
              |           |
  bottom-left |           | bottom-right
              ∨           ∨
              e --------> f
                 bottom
```

and consider a homotopy `K : f ~ g`. Then the right whiskering of the vertical
pasting of the two squares above with `K` is up to associativity the vertical
pasting of the squares

```text
                     top
              a ------------> b
              |               |
     top-left |               | top-right
              ∨    middle     ∨
              c ------------> d
              |               |
  bottom-left |               | bottom-right ∙h K
              ∨               ∨
              e ------------> g.
                 bottom ∙h K
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="49812" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="49819" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#49819" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="49823" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="49824" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#49824" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="49827" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#49827" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="49830" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="49832" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="49837" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="49839" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="49840" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#49840" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="49842" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="49844" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="49847" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#49824" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="49849" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="49851" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="49852" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#49852" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="49854" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="49856" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#49840" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="49858" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="49860" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="49863" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#49827" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="49865" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="51189" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51189" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="51193" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51193" class="Bound">top-left</a> <a id="51202" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51202" class="Bound">top-right</a> <a id="51212" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51212" class="Bound">middle</a> <a id="51219" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51219" class="Bound">bottom-left</a> <a id="51231" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51231" class="Bound">bottom-right</a> <a id="51244" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51244" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="51251" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51251" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="51253" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51253" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="51255" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51255" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="51257" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51257" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="51259" class="Symbol">=</a>

      <a id="51481" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="51483" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51251" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="51485" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51257" class="Bound">x</a><a id="51486" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="51494" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="51496" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51253" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="51498" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51257" class="Bound">x</a><a id="51499" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="51507" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="51509" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51255" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="51511" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-homotopies.html#51257" class="Bound">x</a><a id="51512" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
